    id integer NOT NULL,
    descripcion character varying NOT NULL,
    estatus integer DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
    created_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL,
    updated_at timestamp without time zone NOT NULL
);

    INCREMENT BY 1
